     "source": [
      "Hip and Jack Rafter Cut Information"
     ]
    },
    {
     "cell_type": "markdown",
     "metadata": {},
     "source": [
      "This IPython Notebook contains calculations on what angle and bevel to set a compound miter saw make a cheek cut where\n",
      "a hip rafter connects to a ridge board and jack rafters connects to a hip rafter.  These calculatins do NOT assume that\n",
      "both the front roof and side roof are at the same pitch.\n",
      "\n",
      "The final output contains the saw angles and bevels needed to cut following results:\n",
      "\n",
      "* Hip rafter angle\n",
      "* Hip rafter cheek cut bevel angle\n",
      "* Front roof cheek cut bevel angle\n",
      "* Side roof cheek cut bevel angle\n",
      "\n",
      "As a check the pitch of the hip rafter is also calculated.\n",
      "\n",
      "*Images are for name clarification*\n",
      "\n",
      "###(Summary is at the bottom.)"
     ]
    },
    {
     "cell_type": "code",
     "collapsed": false,
     "input": [
      "from IPython.display import Image\n",
      "Image(url='http://i.imgur.com/sTI9YHq.png')"
     ],
     "language": "python",
     "metadata": {},
     "outputs": [

      "####This notebook uses the py2tex extension to display all the calculations with the %%tex magic.\n",
      "####Using %%tex is not necessary for the operation of the notebook, it is just for equation verification and claity.\n",
      "* py2tex can be downloaded from the [Extensions-Index](https://github.com/ipython/ipython/wiki/Extensions-Index)\n",
      "* The necessity of py2tex can be removed by deleting all instances of %%tex and %load py2tex."
     ]
    },
    {
     "cell_type": "code",
     "collapsed": false,
     "input": [
      "%load_ext py2tex\n",
      "\n",
      "rad = radians\n",
      "deg = degrees\n",
      "\n",
      "%%tex front_pitch = 4 # inches per foot of run of the front roof\n",
      "%%tex side_pitch = 6 # inches per foot of run of the side roof\n",
      "%%tex front_angle = deg(arctan(front_pitch/12))\n",
      "%%tex side_angle = deg(arctan(side_pitch/12))"
     ],
     "language": "python",
     "metadata": {},
     "outputs": [
      {
       "latex": [
        "$$\\mbox{front}_{pitch} = 4 = 4.000$$"
       ],
       "output_type": "display_data",
       "text": [
        "front_pitch = 4 # inches per foot of run of the front roof = 4.000"
       ]
      },
      {
       "latex": [
        "$$\\mbox{side}_{pitch} = 6 = 6.000$$"
       ],
       "output_type": "display_data",
       "text": [
        "side_pitch = 6 # inches per foot of run of the side roof = 6.000"
       ]
      },
      {
       "latex": [
        "$$\\mbox{front}_{angle} = \\mbox{deg}\\left(\\arctan\\left(\\frac{front_{pitch}}{12}\\right)\\right) = 18.435$$"
       ],
       "output_type": "display_data",
       "text": [
        "front_angle = deg(arctan(front_pitch/12)) = 18.435"
       ]
      },
      {
       "latex": [
        "$$\\mbox{side}_{angle} = \\mbox{deg}\\left(\\arctan\\left(\\frac{side_{pitch}}{12}\\right)\\right) = 26.565$$"
       ],
       "output_type": "display_data",
       "text": [
        "side_angle = deg(arctan(side_pitch/12)) = 26.565"
       ]
      }
     ],
     "prompt_number": 2

    {
     "cell_type": "code",
     "collapsed": false,
     "input": [
      "%%tex side_run = front_pitch * (12 / side_pitch) #this is the run the side roof jack rafter must have to match 12\" of run of the front roof\n",
      "hip_run = sqrt(side_run**2 + 12**2) #this is the run the hip rafter mut have for every 12\" of run of the fron roof\n",
      "hipUnit_length = sqrt(front_pitch**2 + hip_run**2) #unit length of a hip rafter per 1 ft of run of the front roof \n",
      "hip_angle = deg(arcsin(front_pitch/hipUnit_length)) #this is angle of the hip rafter\n",
      "hip_pitch = front_pitch * (12 / hip_run) #this is the rise of the hip rafter for every 12\" of hip run"
     ],
     "language": "python",
     "metadata": {},
     "outputs": [
      {
       "latex": [
        "$$\\mbox{side}_{run} = front_{pitch} \\cdot \\frac{12}{side_{pitch}} = 8.000$$"
       ],
       "output_type": "display_data",
       "text": [
        "side_run = front_pitch * (12 / side_pitch) #this is the run the side roof jack rafter must have to match 12\" of run of the front roof = 8.000"
       ]
      },
      {
       "latex": [
        "$$\\mbox{hip}_{run} = \\sqrt{side_{run}^{2} + 12^{2}} = 14.422$$"
       ],
       "output_type": "display_data",
       "text": [
        "hip_run = sqrt(side_run**2 + 12**2) #this is the run the hip rafter mut have for every 12\" of run of the fron roof = 14.422"
       ]
      },
      {
       "latex": [
        "$$\\mbox{hipUnit}_{length} = \\sqrt{front_{pitch}^{2} + hip_{run}^{2}} = 14.967$$"
       ],
       "output_type": "display_data",
       "text": [
        "hipUnit_length = sqrt(front_pitch**2 + hip_run**2) #unit length of a hip rafter per 1 ft of run of the front roof  = 14.967"
       ]
      },
      {
       "latex": [
        "$$\\mbox{hip}_{angle} = \\mbox{deg}\\left(\\arcsin\\left(\\frac{front_{pitch}}{hipUnit_{length}}\\right)\\right) = 15.501$$"
       ],
       "output_type": "display_data",
       "text": [
        "hip_angle = deg(arcsin(front_pitch/hipUnit_length)) #this is angle of the hip rafter = 15.501"
       ]
      },
      {
       "latex": [
        "$$\\mbox{hip}_{pitch} = front_{pitch} \\cdot \\frac{12}{hip_{run}} = 3.328$$"
       ],
       "output_type": "display_data",
       "text": [
        "hip_pitch = front_pitch * (12 / hip_run) #this is the rise of the hip rafter for every 12\" of hip run = 3.328"
       ]
      }

      "print(\"The angle the hip rafter makes with the house projected into the horizontal plane is:\")\n",
      "%%tex HipCheekProj_angle = deg(arccos(side_run/hip_run)) #this is the angle the hip rafter makes with the house projected into the horizontal plane\n",
      "print(\"\\nlength_projection is the projection of this length_actual into the horizontal plane. The 1.5 is based on 2x material being used for the rafter.\")\n",
      "%%tex length_projection = 1.5 / tan(rad(HipCheekProj_angle)) # length_projection is the projection of this l_act into the horizontal plane. The 1.5 is based on 2x material being used the rafter\n",
      "print(\"\\nHip_rise is the rise of the hip rafter up the rake for the distance length_actual\")\n",
      "%%tex Hip_rise = hip_pitch /12 *length_projection # Hip_rise is the rise of the hip rafter up the rake for the distance l_act\n",
      "print(\"\\nlength_actual is the length down the rake of the hip rafter from the tip to the end of the cheek cut on the starting edge\")\n",
      "%%tex length_actual = sqrt(length_projection**2 + Hip_rise**2) # length_actual is the length down the rake of the hip rafter from the tip to the end of the cheek cut on the starting edge\n",
      "%%tex hipCheekCut_angle = deg(arctan(length_actual/1.5)) #this is the angle of the saw\n",

     "input": [
      "def saw_cheek_cut(projected_angle, rafter_pitch):\n",
      "    \"\"\"This function allows me to calculate multiple jack rafter miter angles.\"\"\"\n",
      "    lR_pro = 1.5 / tan(rad(projected_angle)) # lR_pro is the projection of this lR_act into the horizontal plane\n",
      "    lR_ri = rafter_pitch /12 *lR_pro # lR_ri is the rise of the rafter up the rake for the distance lR_act\n",
      "    lR_act = sqrt(lR_pro**2 + lR_ri**2) # lR_act is the length down the rake of the rafter from the tip to the end of the cheek cut on the starting edge\n",
      "    CheekCut_angle = deg(arctan(lR_act/1.5))\n",
      "    return CheekCut_angle"
     ],
     "language": "python",
     "metadata": {},
     "outputs": [],
     "prompt_number": 7
    },
    {
     "cell_type": "heading",
     "level": 2,
     "metadata": {},
     "source": [
      "In summary:"
     ]
    },
    {
     "cell_type": "code",
     "collapsed": false,
     "input": [
      "from fractions import Fraction as frac\n",
      "inch_part = floor(hip_pitch)\n",
      "frac_part = round((hip_pitch - inch_part)*16)/16\n",
      "hip_pitch_sum = ('The pitch of the hip rafter (rise over 12 inches) is: {:.0f}-{}\"'.format(inch_part, frac.from_float(frac_part)))\n",
      "hip_angle_sum = (\"The angle equivalent of the hip rafter's pitch is {:.1f} degrees\".format(hip_angle))\n",
      "hip_cheek_sum=('The bevel of the saw for the cheek cut of the hip rafter is {0:.1f} degrees'.format(hipCheekCut_angle))\n",
      "\n",
      "inch_part = floor(front_pitch)\n",
      "frac_part = round((front_pitch - inch_part)*16)/16\n",
      "FrontjackRafter_sum = ('The pitch of the front jack rafter (rise over 12 inches) is: {:.0f}-{}\"'.format(inch_part, frac.from_float(frac_part)))\n",
      "Front_angle_sum = (\"The angle equivalent of the front jack rafter's pitch is {:.1f} degrees\".format(front_angle))\n",
      "FrontjackCheekCut_angle = saw_cheek_cut(deg(arccos(12/hip_run)), front_pitch)\n",
      "front_jack_sum = ('The bevel of the saw for the cheek cut of a front roof jack rafter is {0:.1f} degrees'.format(FrontjackCheekCut_angle))\n",
      "\n",
      "inch_part = floor(side_pitch)\n",
      "frac_part = round((side_pitch - inch_part)*16)/16\n",
